175b2(phal chen): de gzungs de dag la sogs pa gzungs kyi sgo brgya stong grangs med pa phrag bcu yongs su tshangs par thob ste/ gzungs kyi sgo brgya stong grangs med pa phrag bcu dang ldan pa'i dbyangs kyi yan lag la mkhas pas
175b3(phal chen): de snyed du tshad med pa nyid dang ldan pa'i spobs pa rnam par bye ba'i sgos chos ston to/ / de de ltar tshad med pa'i gzungs kyi sgo brgya stong grangs med pas tshad med pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams las
175b4(phal chen): chos nyan cing thos nas kyang brjed par mi byed de/ / ji skad du thos pa'ang tshad med par rnam par phye bas shin tu ston to// de ni de bzhin gshegs pa gcig las gzungs kyi sgo brgya stong grangs med
175b5(phal chen): pa phrag bcus chos khong du chud par byed de/ de bzhin gshegs pa gcig las ji lta ba de bzhin du yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mtha' yas pa las gzungs kyi sgo brgya stong grangs med pa phrag
175b6(phal chen): bcus chos khong du chud par byed do/ / de smon pa tsam gyis kyang yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams las chos kyi sgo snang ba ches mang du yang dag par 'dzin gyi/ nyan thos shin tu mang du thos
175b7(phal chen): pa dang ldan pa zos pa 'dzin pa'i gzungs rab tu thob pa rnams kyis ni bskal pa brgya phrag stong du'ang gzung ba'i byor gyi rlabs kyis de ltar mi zin to/ / de ltar de lta bu'i gzungs thob cing
176a1(phal chen): spobs pa thob pas chos kyi gtam bya ba'i phyir 'dug na/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/ chos kyi stan la 'dug cing sems
176a2(phal chen): can rnams la bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par phye zhing chos ston to/ / de'i chos kyi stan yang de bzhin gshegs pa dag dang / byang chub sems dpa' dbang bskur ba'i sa thob pa ma gtogs par thams
176a3(phal chen): cad las 'phags shing snang ba tshad med pa dang ldan pa yin/ de 'dod na chos kyi stan la 'dug cing dbyangs gcig gis 'khor thams cad du sgra skad sna tshogs rnam pa tha dad pas yang dag par go bar
176a4(phal chen): byed do/ / 'dod na sgra skad sna tshogs dang / dbyangs kyi yan lag tha dad pa rnam par phye bas/ 'khor thams cad mngon par go bar byed do// 'dod na 'od zer gyi sgo nye bar bsgrubs pas/ chos kyi sgo
176a5(phal chen): shin tu brjod do/ / 'dod na ba spu'i bu ga thams cad nas dbyangs rnam par phye ba shin tu brjod do// 'dod na stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams na gzugs su snang ba ji snyed yod pa'i
176a6(phal chen): gzugs su snang ba de dag las chos kyi sgra 'byung bar byed do/ / 'dod na dbyangs kyi yan lag gcig gi sgras chos kyi dbyings thams cad khong du rung bar byed do// 'dod na sgra dang dbyangs thams cad chos
176a7(phal chen): kyi sgrar byin gyis rlob bo/ / 'dod na 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad yod pa'i glu dang / rol mo brdung ba dang / dkrol ba'i sgra thams cad las chos kyi sgra 'byung bar byed do// 'dod na yi ge gcig gi sgra
176b1(phal chen): las chos thams cad kyi tshig rab tu phye ba'i sgra 'byung bar byed do/ / 'dod na 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' yas shing brjod du med pa'i sa dang / chu dang / me dang / rlung kyi phung po rdul shin tu phra rab rnam par phye ba'i
176b2(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba re re las chos kyi sgo brjod du med pa 'byung bar byed do/ / gal te de la stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams su gtogs pa'i sems can rnams 'ongs te/ skad cig yun
176b3(phal chen): tsam zang cig tu dri ba yongs su 'dri zhing / de dag re res kyang sgra rnam pa tha dad pa tshad med pas yongs su dris par gyur la/ gcig gis gang dris pa de gzhan mi 'dri bar gyur na'ang de la byang chub
176b4(phal chen): sems dpa' des sems can de dag thams cad kyi sgra tshig so so dang / yi ge'i 'bru yan chad ma lus par bzung ste/ bzung nas kyang tshig gcig mngon par brjod pas sems can de dag thams cad
176b5(phal chen): kyi sems dang bsam pa tshim par byed pa nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa'i bar du gtogs pa'i sems can thams cad kyi skad cig zang cig yud tsam du dri ba yongs su dris te/ de dag re re zhing
176b6(phal chen): yang sgra rnam pa tha dad pa tshad med pas 'dri bar gyur la/ gcig gis ci dris pa de gzhan mi 'dri bar gyur na'ang / de dag thams cad byang chub sems dpa' des skad cig yud tsam thang cig tu ma lus par
176b7(phal chen): bzung ste/ sgra gcig brjod pas de dag thams cad khong du chud par byed do// de 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bar dag kyang rgyas par bkang zhing sems can rnams la bsam
177a1(phal chen): pa dang / dbang po dang / mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du chos ston to// chos kyi gtam la zhugs pa'i tshe'ang de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi rlabs len cing sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa thams
177a2(phal chen): cad kyis sems can thams cad la nye bar gnas pa yin/ yang de 'di lta bu'i ye shes snang bas 'dzin pa yongs su rtsom ste/ gal te sgra'i rtse mo'i go gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa'i rdul
177a3(phal chen): shin tu phra ba ji snyed pa de snyed kyi de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs la/ de skad du tshad med par gyur pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du chos bstanate/ de bzhin gshegs pa de dag re res kyang / de snyed kyi sems can chud
177a4(phal chen): med pa la chos rnam pa tha dad par shin tu bstan te/ sems can gyi bsam pa'i rgyud re re la'ang de skad du chos nye bar bsgrub pa tshad med par nye bar bsgrub par gyur la/ de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gis ji lta ba
177a5(phal chen): bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad du ste/ skra'i rtse mo'i go gcig la ji lta ba de bzhin du chos kyi dbyings thams cad du de ltar gyur kyang de dag thams cad zin
177a6(phal chen): par gyur na/ 'jig rten gyi khams de tsam dag gi sems can rnams kyi lta smos kyang ci dgos/ de de ltar byang chub sems dpa'i sa legs pa'i blo gros 'di thob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni nyin mtshan
177a7(phal chen): du yid la bsam pa gzhan med par sangs rgyas kyi spyod yul la zhugs pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa dang 'grogs pa rab tu thob cing byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa zab mo rab tu thob pa yin/ de de lta bu'i//
177b1(phal chen): ye shes dang ldan zhing mnyam par bzhag kyang de bzhin gshegs pa blta ba yongs su mi spong ste/ bskal pa re re zhing yang sangs rgyas du ma nas/ sangs rgyas brgya stong bye ba khrag khrig lta zhing mthong nas kyang rim
177b2(phal chen): gro dang / bkur sti dang / bsti sbrang dang / mchod pa byed de/ sangs rgyas mthong zhing mchod pa bya ba rgya chen po yongs su mi gtong ngo // de bzhin gshegs pa de dag la zhu ba yongs su bu ba'ang byed de/ cho
177b3(phal chen): kyi gzungs rab tu bstan pa las shin tu byung ba yin/ de'i dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag kyang ston pas kyang shin tu byang zhing mi 'phrogs par 'gyur te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di lta ste
177b4(phal chen): dper na gser gyi sa le sbram de nyid mgar ba mkhas pas rgyan du byas te/ yongs su zin pa 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po'i yan lag gi dam pa mgo 'am mgul du btags na/ khams kyi rgyal po
177b5(phal chen): thams cad dang gling bzhi pa'i sems can thams cad kyi rgyan gyi rnam pas mi thub cing mi 'phrogs pa yin no/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i sa legs pa'i blo gros 'di la gnas
177b6(phal chen): pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag kyang nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas dang / sa 'og ma la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyis mi 'phrogs shing mi thub pa yin//
177b7(phal chen): de'i dge ba'i rtsa ba des ni sems can rnams kyi nyon mongs pa dang / sems kyi thibs po snang bar byas te de nyid nas phyir ldog go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di lta ste/ dper na stong gnyis la dbang ba'i
178a1(phal chen): tshangs pa chen po ni stong gnyis kyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi thibs po dma' bar gzhol ba yongs su snang bar byed do/ / kye rgyal ba'i zas dag/ de bzhin du byang chub sems
178a2(phal chen): dpa'i sa legs pa'i blo gros 'di la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba snang ba de'ang sems can rnams kyi nyon mongs pa dang / sems kyi thibs po snang bar byas te/ de nyid nas phyir ldog
178a3(phal chen): gode'i pha rol tu phyin pa bcu las stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i shas che ba yin te/ lhag ma rnams kyang ci tshul ci nus su yang dag par mi sgrub par ni ma yin no// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag
178a4(phal chen): 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i sa legs pa'i blo gros shes bya ba ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa dgu pa mdor bstan pa'o// rgya cher ni bskal pa mu med pa'i bstan pa'i mthar thug par shes
178a5(phal chen): par bya'o/ / de la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni phal cher tshangs pa chen por gyur te/ stobs dang mthu chen po thob pa stong gnyis la dbang zhing zil gyis gnon la
178a6(phal chen): gzhan gyis zil gyis mi nor pa/ mthun pa'i don mthong ba/ dbang shin tu thob pa/ sems can rnams la nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa'i pha rol tu phyin pa
178a7(phal chen): thams cad ston pa la mkhas shing mthu yod pa de/ sems can gyi bsam pa yongs su dris pa bstan pas mi 'phrogs pa yin// de sbyin pa 'am/ ngag snyan pa 'am/ don bsgrub pa 'am/ don
178b1(phal chen): mthun pas dge ba'i rtsa ba gang ci rtsom yang rung ste/ de thams cad ji ltar na sems can thams cad kyi mchog tu 'gyur/ gtso bor 'gyur/ thu bor 'gyur/ phul du 'gyur/ dam par 'gyur
178b2(phal chen): bla na med par 'gyur/ 'dren par 'gyur/ yongs su 'dren par 'gyur ba nas/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la rten pa'i bar du 'gyur snyam ste/ sangs rgyas yid la bya ba dang / chos yin
178b3(phal chen): la bya ba dang / dge 'dun yid la bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' yid la bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yid la bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sa yid la bya ba dang / pha rol tu phyin pa yid
178b4(phal chen): la bya ba dang / stobs yid la bya ba dang / mi 'jigs pa yid la bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa yid la bya ba nas/ rnam pa'i mchog thams cad dang ldan pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes
178b5(phal chen): kyi bar du yid la bya ba dang mi 'bral ba yin te/ de 'dod na skad cig yud tsam thang cig tu ting nge 'dzin sangs rgyas kyi zhing grangs med pa brgya stong phrag bcu chung ba'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rab tu thob cing de dag
178b6(phal chen): la snyoms par 'jug pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing grangs med pa brgya stong phrag bcu tshang ba'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed mthong ba dang / de dag gi byin gyi rlabs kyang yang dag par shes pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams
178b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi zhing grangs med pa brgya stong phrag bcu tshang ba'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed skyod pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing grangs med pa brgya stong phrag bcu tshang ba'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du 'gro ba dang / 'jig rten gyi
179a1(phal chen): / khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing grangs med pa brgya stong phrag bcu tshang ba'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed snang bar bya ba dang / sems can sangs rgyas kyi zhing grangs med pa brgya stong phrag bcu chang
179a2(phal chen): ba'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed yongs su smin par bya ba dang / bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing grangs med pa brgya stong phrag bcu tshang ba'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du gnas par bya ba dang / sngon gyi mnga' dang phyi ma'i
179a3(phal chen): mtha'i bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing grangs med pa brgya stong phrag bcu tshang ba'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la rab tu 'jug pa dang / chos kyi sgo sangs rgyas kyi zhing grangs med pa brgya stong phrag bcu tshang ba'i rdul
179a4(phal chen): shin tu phra ba snyed rnam par 'byed pa dang / lus sangs rgyas kyi zhing grangs med pa brgya stong phrag bcu tshang ba'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed yongs su bstan pa dang / lus re re'ang byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor sangs rgyas kyi
179a5(phal chen): zhing grangs med pa brgya stong phrag bcu tshang ba'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed yang dag par bstan pa'i brtson 'grus kyi rnam pa de lta bu rtsom mo/ / de yan rang byang chub sems dpa' smon lam gyi mthu can rnams smon lam gyi khyad par
179a6(phal chen): gyis rnam par 'phrul te/ de dag gi lus sam/ 'od dam/ rdzu 'phrul lam/ mig gam/ spyod yul lam/ dbyangs sam/ spyod pa 'am/ rgyan tam/ byin gyi rlabs sam/ mos pa 'am/ mngon par 'du byed pa
179a7(phal chen): dag kyang bskal pa du ma dang / bskal pa brgya phrag du ma dang / bskal pa stong phrag du ma dang / bskal pa brgya stong phrag du ma dang / bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag du mas kyang bgrang bar dka' 'o//
179b1(phal chen): de nas kyang chub sems dpa' 'a cha dang thos pa ngon 'ang bdags par bya ba dang / bstan par bya ra gyur de'i tshetshams sung bdang 'dir gasmras so// de dag ra me thobs pa
179b2(phal chen): yis rnam dpyod cing / / ye shes phra ba'i dam pa 'gro bas shes dkar ba// de bzhin dade gshegs gsang ba'i gnas la yang dag 'jug/ 'gro ba'i don byed de dgas dgu yongs su gnon//
179b3(phal chen): de dag gzungs mchog ting 'dzin che ba nyid mchog dang // mngon shes yang sa dang de bzhin zhing 'jug mtha' yas dang // stobs dang rtogs pa'i ye shes rgyal ba'i brtan gnas dang // smon lam
179b4(phal chen): snying rje'i bsam pas mkhas pa dgu la 'jug/ sa dgu ldan pa de dag rgyal ba'i mdzod 'dzin cing // dge ba'i chos dang mi dge lung du ma bstan dang // zag dang bcas dang 'jig rten pa dang 'phags
179b5(phal chen): pa dang / / bsam du rung dang bsam du mi rung mkhas pas shes// nges pa'i chos dang ma nges ros kyang rab tu rtogs// theg gsum phun sum tshogs pa'i bya ba yongs su 'jal// 'dus byas rnam
179b6(phal chen): par phye dang grangs dang rgyu ba dag/ 'jig rten ji ltar mngon byed de la rab tu 'jug/ de dag de 'dra'i shes ldan blo mchog phra ldan pa// sems can sems kyi thibs po yongs su rtog pa byed//
179b7(phal chen): rnam shes sna tshogs myur du 'gyur zhing ldog pa dang / rnam shes mtha' yas 'byung la rtag tu mkhas pa 'jug/ nyon mongs mtha' yas sbyor dang grogs su 'gyur ba dang // kun nas 'khor dang
180a1(phal chen): bag nyal 'gro rgyud mtshams sbyor dang / / las rnams sna tshogs rnam par phye la'ang de bzhin 'jug/ rgyu dang 'gog dang de bzhin 'bras bu 'jig la'ang yang dag 'jug/ dbang po
180a2(phal chen): rno dang tha ma 'bring dang yangs pa dang / / tha dad sngon dang phyi ma'i mtha' la'ang yang dag 'jug/ mos pa dge dang mi dge sna tshogs du ma dag/ stong phrag brgyad cu rtsa bzhi kun la yang dag 'jug/ khams kyi
180a3(phal chen): rnam pa nyon mongs lta ba srid pa'i rnams/ / thibs por gyur pa snga phyi med cing 'chad med dang // bag nyal bsam pa lhan cig skyes pa'i rgyud rnams kyi// sems rnams kun rgyu 'brel cing rgyun 'chad mi
180a4(phal chen): 'gyur ba/ / bsam pa bag nyal rgyud yod dngos po ma yin te// yul la mi gnas bsam pa yongs su 'a bral mi 'gyur// shes pa dka' ba'i bsam gtan yul las phyir mi ldog/ rdo rje lta bu'i lam gyis chod
180a5(phal chen): 'gyur gzhan gyis min/ / rgyud drug skye ba rnam par phye la rab tu 'jug/ sred rlan ma rig mun pa de bzhi las kyi zhing // rnam shes sa bon can 'gyur myu gu ming dang gzugs// khams gsum sngon mtha' med par
180a6(phal chen): de dag rab tu 'jug/ de dag bag chags tshul dang nyon mongs las dang sems// 'dod chags bral bas lam gyi rgyud du 'byung ba min// sems can phung po gsum du nges pa yang dag lta bar bying ba shes pa'i las
180a7(phal chen): dang de dag ldan/ / de 'dra'i shes ldan sa mchog 'di la gnas pa ste// sems can bsam pa mos pa dbang po'i tshul bzhin du// chos rnams rnam par phye zhing shin tu ston pa byed// rnga dang yang dag don
180b1(phal chen): shes nges tshig spobs pa yin/ / de dag chos smra'i tshul la gnas pa rab tu thob// seng ge khyu mchog dpe' dra ri yi rgyal po 'dra// bdud rtsi sprin chen zhim pa'i char yang rab tu 'bebs// klu yi dbang po
180b2(phal chen): rgya mtsho rgyas pa byed pa bzhin/ / don gyi don shes de bzhin chos nyid rab tu shes// nges tshig rjes su song zhing spobs pa rab tu thob// de dag grangs med stong phrag bcu yi gzungs thob pas// chos rnams/
180b3(phal chen): radzin pa rgya mtsho sprin chen char 'dzin bzhin// de dag de 'dra'i ting 'dzin gzungs gsal thob gyur par// skad cig gcig gis sangs rgyas mang po stong yang mthong // rin chen chos rnams thos nas
180b4(phal chen): yang du ston byed de/ / tshig gi dkyil 'khor rnam dag dbyangs kyi yan lag ldan// 'dod na stong gsum 'jig rten khams su gtogs pa yi// sems can bsam sems sna tshogs tshul bzhin smin byed cing // /

180b6(phal chen): gyis mi khyab sems pa byed/ / sems can sna tshogs mngal ba de gshegs chos ston pa// thos nas sa bon kun 'dzin sa gzhi yongs su 'dzin// phyogs rnams bcu po'i sems can mang po rdza
180b7(phal chen): snyed pa/ / de dag thams cad 'khor gcig 'dus par 'khod gyur kyang // de dag bsam pa skad cig gcig gis bsam byas shing // sgra skad gcig gis de dag thams cad tshim par byed/
181a1(phal chen): 'di la gnas pa chos rgyal lha mi mchog du 'gyur// rngul pa'i zas po chos kyis yongs su sbyong ba yin// nyin ma can kun tu rgyal ba rnams dang rtag byang 'grogs/ chub sangs
181a2(phal chen): ye shes rnam par thar pa ldan par gnas/ / de dag yang du sangs rgyas khrag khrig bsnyen bkur byed// 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyan bzang yongs su byang ba bzhin// de yi 'od kyang nyon mongs thibs po snang ba
181a3(phal chen): byed/ tshangs pa'i 'od kyis stong gnyis 'jig rten ji bzhin no// 'di la gnas pa legs ldan tshangs chen 'jig rten du// skye 'gyur theg gsum ston la mkhas shing mthu yod pa// 'gro ba
181a4(phal chen): kun la phan phyir ci rtsom gang yang rung / / yon tan shes ldan pa de gshegs ye shes ldan pa sngo// grangs med zhing du gtogs pa'i rdul phran du yod pa// de snyed ting 'dzin skad cig gcig tu brtan
181a5(phal chen): bathob/ / phyogs rnams kun gyi rgyal ba mthong zhing gsung yang nyan// yan chad smon lam ldan pa tshad med rnam par 'phrul// 'di ni sa rab dgu pa ste/ ye shes chen pos rnam par spyod// zab cing blta dka'
181a6(phal chen): shin tu za/ / rgyal ba'i sras kyis bstan pa yin// legs pa'i blo zos shes bya ba ste byang chub sems dpa'i sa dgu pa'o// bam po lnga bcu gnyis pa/
181a7(phal chen): spyod pa bla na med pa 'di thos nas// gtsang gnas lha rnams bye ba rab tu dga'// dbang po tshim par bar snang mkha' la gnas/ bde bar gshegs la rje sar mchod pa byed// byang chub sems dpa'
181b1(phal chen): bye ba bsam yas pa/ / bar snang mkha' gnas rab tu dgar gyur cing // spos sprin tshad med yid du 'ong ba dag/ 'gro ba'i nyon mongs sel ba dri zhim 'dug pa byed// lha yi dbang po dbang sgyur rab dgar
181b2(phal chen): zhing / rnga bar snang gnas las lha 'khor khrag khrig dang // rim gro bcas par gos rnams 'dor bar byed// yid 'ong gos brgya yongs su bskor ba byas// lha yi bu mo mang po shin tu dga'//
181b3(phal chen): bde bar gshegs la rjesas mchod pa byed// rol mo brdung ba bye ba khrag khrig byed// 'di 'dra'i sgra dbyangs kun las byung bar 'gyur// zhing mchog gcig na bde bar gshegs pa bzhugs//
181b4(phal chen): zhing rnams kun tu sku gzugs rab tu bstan// sku gzugs khrag khrig sna tshogs yid du 'ong // chos dbyings rgya chen yongs su rgyas par gang // spu gcig rtse nas bde gshegs 'od bkye ba/
181b5(phal chen): 'gro ba'i nyon mongs yongs su zhi bar 'phro// zhing gi rdul khams zad par nus 'gyur gyi// de dag bgrang bas shes par mi nus so// la las sangs rgyas mtshan rab mngar bar mthong // 'khor los

250a3(phal chen): gnas pa dang / ting nge 'dzin thams cad la mi gnas pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad la mi gnas pa dang / sa thams cad la mi gnas pa ste/ byang chub sems dpa' lus pang
250a4(phal chen): dag par 'dres pa'i ting nge 'dzin la gnas pa'i tshe/ gnas med pa bcu po 'di dag rab tu 'thob bo// / bam po lnga bcu rtsa mdun pa/ ji ltaran

257a6(phal chen): ldang bar ston to/ / skal ba mi mnyam pa la snyoms par zhugs shing / skal ba mnyam pa las rnam par ldang bar ston to// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'di lta
257a7(phal chen): ste/ dper na lha dang lha ma yin g.yul du lhag pa'i tshe/ lha rnams rgyal zhing lha ma yin pham par gyur na/ de'i tshe lha'i dbang po dpag tshad brgya'i lus mig stong dang ldan pa dpung gi tsheg/
257b1(phal chen): yan lag bzhis yongs su bskor cing / lha ma yin rnams 'thor te/ de'i tshe lha ma yin gyi dbang po de lha ma yin gyi sbru la shin tu mkhas pas/ sum cu rtsa sum mamapa'i lha'i sde
257b2(phal chen): kun tu 'byer ba dang / rdzing bde ba 'byung ba'i drung gi khung nas lha ma yin shing rta dang / bzhon pa dang / dpung du bcas pa mang po 'byung bar ston to// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de bzhin

257b7(phal chen): la las yongs su dag pa ni yan lag dang nying lag thams cad dang ldan pa dbang po tshang zhing rnam par dag par skye'ang khrag bsdus pa de'ang gzhan/ dbang po drug rnams kyang gzhan no// khrag
258a1(phal chen): bsdus pa de la'ang dbang po drug phra ba'i tshul du med pa ma yin te/ srid pa'i yan lag gi mtshan nyid dang ldan la las gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pas bskyed cing rlung
258a2(phal chen): dang ldan na las kyi rnam par smin pa ji lta ba bzhin yan lag ma nyams par skye'o/ / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang thams cad mkhyen pa'i dngos po'i tshul du snyoms par zhugs shing / dngos
258a3(phal chen): bopo med pa'i tshul las rnam par ldang ngo / / 'di lta ste/ dper na klu'i gnas ni sa la rten mod kyi/ bar sdang gnas la sprin kyang skyed la/ bar snang gnas la klu'i gnas dang khyim med kyang sprin
258a4(phal chen): gyi char 'dod pa'i mi rnams gyen du lta zhing / klu'i sprul pa bar snang gi gnas la yod pa la lta ste/ gnas 'og na 'dug kyang sprin bla na lding bar snang ngo // de bzhin du ting nge 'dzin 'di thob pa'i
258a5(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' mtshan nyid med pa la snyoms par zhugs shing / mtshan nyid las rnam par ldang ngo // 'di lta ste/ dper na tshangs pa yid du 'ong ba zhes bya ba'i tshangs pa'i
258a6(phal chen): gzhal med khang chen po rnam dag phul zhes bya ba yod de/ gzhal med khang chen po de la stong gi 'jig rten thams cad snang ngo // stong phrag bcu'i 'jig rten thams cad snang ngo // stong phrag

258b6(phal chen): ba'i gzegs ma bar snang gnas la 'phyo ba lta bur phra ba dang / rab dang / chu klung langs pa de dag thams cad kyang / tshangs pa'i gzhal med khang 'gro ba thams cad na bul du gyur

330a4(phal chen): tha dad pa med pa'i tshul gyis ngo bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi stobs thams cad la 'jug go/ nam mkha' ji lta ba de ltar sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha' dang / da ltar byung
330a5(phal chen): ba'i tshul gyis bsam gtan thams cad la rab tu 'jug go/ / nam mkha' ji lta ba de ltar brjod du med pa'i tshul gyis chos thams cad yang dag par bstan pa la 'jug go// nam mkha'
330a6(phal chen): ji lta ba de ltar chags pa med cing bsgribs pa med pa'i tshul gyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku la 'jug go/ / nam mkha' ji lta ba de ltar nam mkha' dbyings kyi tshul gyis chos
330a7(phal chen): thams cad gsal ba med pa la 'jug go/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po nam mkha' lta bu'i chos thams cad la de lta bu'i bzod pa las byung ba'i ye shes kyi
330b1(phal chen): 'jug pa'i tshe/ lus nam mkha' lta bur rab tu 'thob bo// nam mkha' lta bu'i lus kyi las rab tu 'thob po// nam mkha' lta bu'i ngag rab tu 'thob bo// nam mkha' lta bu'i ngag gi las rab tu 'thob
330b2(phal chen): bo/ nam mkha' lta bu'i yid rab tu 'thob bo// nam mkha' lta bu'i yid kyi las rab tu 'thob bo// 'di ste ste/ dper na nam mkha' ni chos thams cad dang ldan te/ 'chi 'pho ba'ang med do// skye/
330b3(phal chen): ba'ang med do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'ang chos thams cad kyi lus dang ldan te/ 'chi 'pho ba'ang med do// skye ba'ang med do// 'di lta ste/ dper na na ma
330b4(phal chen): mkha' ni gzhi med do/ / tha dad pa med do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'ang chos thams cad shes pa sa gzhi med do// sangs rgyas kyi stobs rnams
330b5(phal chen): dang tha mi dad do/ / 'di lta ste/ dper na nam mkha' ni 'jig rten thams cad kyi gzhi ste/ rang bzhin med pa dang yul med pa'i gzhi'ang ma yin no// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'
330b6(phal chen): sems dpa' chen po'ang chos thams cad kyi gzhi yin te/ chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin med pas gzhi'ang ma yin no// 'di lta ste/ dper na nam mkha' ni skye ba med cing 'gag pa
330b7(phal chen): med kyang 'jig rten thams cad kyi skye ba dang 'gag pa 'dzin to/ / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'ang 'jug pa'ang med/ yongs su rdzogs pa'ang med do// 'jig rten thams cad
331a1(phal chen): kyi rnam par dag pa'ang rab tu ston to/ / 'di lta ste/ dper na nam mkha' ni phyogs kyang ma yin/ phyogs mtshams kyang ma yin te/ phyogs rgya mtsho mtha' yas//
331a2(phal chen): pa la'ang yang dag par gzhol lo// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'ang las kyang ma yin/ rnam par smin pa'ang ma yin te/ las dang rnam par smin pa rgya mtsho'ang yongs su
331a3(phal chen): ston to/ / 'di lta ste/ dper na nam mkha' na lding gi med cing 'dug pa med de/ rnam par phye ba mtha' yas pa'ang yongs su ston to// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'ang sgo
331a4(phal chen): pa'ang med gnas pa'ang med de/ spyod pa rnam par phye ba'ang yongs su ston to// 'di lta ste/ dper na nam mkha' ni kha dog kyang ma yin/ kha dog med pa'ang ma yin te/ kha dog gi rnam pa'ang
331a5(phal chen): yongs su ston to/ / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'ang 'jig rten gyi kha dog kyang ma yin/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i kha dog kyang ma yin te/ kha dog mtha' yas
331a6(phal chen): pa'ang yongs su ston to/ / 'di lta ste/ dper na nam mkha' ni ring du gnas pa'ang ma yin/ yud tsam zhig tu gnas pa'ang ma yin te/ gnas pa dang yongs su gnas pa'ang rab tu ston
331a7(phal chen): to/ / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'ang ring du gnas pa'ang ma yin/ yud tsam zhig tu gnas pa'ang ma yin te/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la gnas pa dang /
331b1(phal chen): yongs su gnas pa'ang rab tu ston to// 'di lta ste/ dper na nAm mkha' ni kun nas nyon mongs par gyur pa'ang med la/ rnam par byang bas rnam par byang bar 'gyur ba'ang med
331b2(phal chen): do/ / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'ang 'jig rten la 'jug pas bsgrubs pa'ang med/ rnam par dag cing btsal bar gyur pa'ang med do// 'di lta ste/ dper na nam
331b3(phal chen): mkha' ni 'jig rten thams cad kyi mngon sum du gyur pa yin te/ 'jig rten thams cad ni nam mkha'i mngon sum du gyur pa ma yin no// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i sems dpa' chen
331b4(phal chen): po'ang chos thams cad la mngon sum du gyur pa ste/ byang chub sems dpa' ni chos thams cad kyi mngon sum du gyur pa ma yin no// 'di lta ste/ dper na nam mkha' ni gnas thams cad la rab
331b5(phal chen): tu gzhol ba yin te/ nam mkha'i mtha' ni yod pa ma yin no// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'ang chos kyi gnas thams cad la gnas te byang chub kyi sems ni mtha' yod
331b6(phal chen): pa ma yin no/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni bdag nyid nam mkha' dang mnyam par bya ste yongs su bsgoms pa dang / rnam par spangs pa dang / shin tu bsgrubs pa dang / mnyam pa nyid du byas pa dang //
331b7(phal chen): rgyud kyi tshul gcig tu byas pa dang / ro gcig tu byas pa dang / tshad gcig tu byas pa dang / nam mkha' lta bur dag pa'i kho dog tu byas pa dang / thams cad du 'gro bar byas pa'i phyir ro//
332a1(phal chen): chos thams cad la yang dag par sems pa dang / khong du chud par byed pa dang / chos thams cad tha mi dad pa rab tu 'thob par byed pa dang / zhing thams cad du
332a2(phal chen): 'gro bar bsgrub pa dang / lus thams cad la gnas med pa yongs su rdzogs par byed pa dang / phyogs thams cad la rmongs pa med pa khong du chud par byed pa dang / stobs thams cad tha
332a3(phal chen): mi dad par bsgrub pa dang / yon tan thams cad yul mtha' yas par yongs su rdzogs par byed pa dang / chos thams cad kyi 'byung gnas rab tu thob par byed pa dang / dpag tu med pa thob
332a4(phal chen): par byed pa dang rdo rje ltar brtan pa la rab tu gzhol ba dang / dbyangs kyi yan lag tshad med pa thams cad mngon par bsgrub pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad du phyin cing chos kyi 'khor lo yongs
332a5(phal chen): su mi gtong ba'i phyir ro/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi nam mkha' lta bu'i bzod pa thob pa ste bcu pa'o//
332a6(phal chen): bzod pa de dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de ni 'gro ba med pa'i tshul du 'gro ba med pa'i lus rab tu 'thob bo// 'gag pa med pa'i tshul du skye ba med pa'i lus
332a7(phal chen): rab tu 'thob bo/ / 'jog pa med pa'i tshul du 'pho ba med pa'i lus rab tu 'thob bo// ji ltar mthong ba ma yin pa'i tshul du bden pa med pa'i lus rab tu 'thob bo// mtshan nyid med pa'i
332b1(phal chen): tshul du mtshan nyid gcig pa'i lus rab tu 'thob bo/ / sangs rgyas kyi stobs tshad med pa'i tshul du tshad med pa'i lusas tu 'thob bo// de bzhin nyid kyi mtshan nyid kyi tshul du mnyam pa nyid kyi
332b2(phal chen): lus rab tu 'thob bo/ / dus gsum mnyam pa nyid khong du chud cing bzod pa'i tshul du tha mi dad pa'i lus rab tu 'thob bo// mnyam pa nyid kyi mog rnam par dag pas bsgribs pa med pa'i tshul
332b3(phal chen): du thams cad du 'gro ba'i lus rab tu 'thob bo/ / chos thams cad ldan pa dang mi ldan pa med pa'i tshu du 'dod chags dang bral ba'i mtha'i lus rab tu 'thob bo// bsod nams zad mi shes pa'i tshul du
332b4(phal chen): nam mkha' ltar mtha' dang mu med pa rab tu 'thob bo/ / chos thams cad nam mkha' lta bu'i rang bzhin gyi mtshan nyid kyis mtshan nyid gcig pa'i tshul chos nyid mnyam pa nyid thob pas zad mi shes
332b5(phal chen): shing thogs ma med pa rab tu 'thob bo/ / nam mkha' ltar thogs pa med pa'i tshul du dbyangs mtha' yas shing tshad med pa rab tu 'thob bo// nam mkha' ltar thams cad la thogs pa med
332b6(phal chen): pa'i tshul du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad la mkhas pa yongs su rdzogs shing rnam par dag pa rab tu 'thob bo/ / nam mkha' ltar rgyun 'chad pa med pa'i tshul du sangs rgyas
332b7(phal chen): kyi chos rgya mtsho gcig nas gcig tu 'thob pa tshad med pa thams cad rab tu 'thob bo/ / nam mkha' ltar tshad med cing mthar thug pa med pa'i tshul du sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad tshad med
333a1(phal chen): pa'i zhing du byin gyis rlob pa rab tu 'thob bo/ / nam mkha' rgya mtsho'i tshul du chos thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul pa rgyun mi 'chad par yang dag par ston
333a2(phal chen): pa'ang yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro/ / nam mkha' ltar 'jig rten thams cad 'dzin pa'i tshul du lus thams cad 'jog pa med cing shin tu brtan pa yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro//
333a3(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi gdung ba thams cad kyis nam mkha' 'tshog par mi 'gyur ba'i tshul du rdo rje ltar sra zhing brtan pa rno ba'i dbang po yongs su 'grub par 'gyur ro// nam mkha' lta bu'i ye shes kyi byon gyi rlabs kyi/
333a4(phal chen): tshul du 'jig rten thams cad rab tu 'dzin pa'i stobs la yang dag par 'byung ngo // kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'di na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi bzod pa thob pa ste bcu pa'o//
333a5(phal chen): de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang pos don de nyid de bas kyang gsal bar bstan pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag la tshigs su bcad de smras pa
333a6(phal chen): ji ltar skyes bu sa la zhig/ rin chen 'byung gnas thos gyur na// nor tshogs chen po bsags don du// rab tu dga' ba skye ba yin// de bzhin shes rab che ldan pa'o// byang chub sems dpa' rgyal sras
333a7(phal chen): rnams/ / de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi mtshan// zab tsang zhi ba rab tu nyan// zab pa'i chos ni thos gyur cing // de dag yi do na 'jigs mi 'gyur// de dag sems la sdang ba med/ skrag pa skye bar
333b1(phal chen): mi 'gyur ro/ / rgya chen dbyangs ni thos gyur nas// bzod pa'i dbyangs kyis byang chub tu// shes rab chen po yang dag 'jug/ de la the tshom skye ba med// bdag ni thams cad mkhyen par bya/
333b2(phal chen): bdag ni mi yi mgon du bya// chos rab shin tu zab pa rnams// bdag gis sgra yi sgo nas thos// sgra po rjes su 'brang bas ni// dga' ba'i dam pa mi 'thob ces//
333b3(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i chos don du// de yi mos pa brtan pa skye// bsam pa byang chub sems rab kyis// 'du shes yongs su sgom par byed// chos rnams
333b4(phal chen): 'khrug par mi byed de/ / de yi dad pa rnam par 'phel// des ni sgra rjes 'gro ba yi// bzod pa rab tu thob par 'gyur// spyod pa shin tu brtson byed cing // dbyangs tu
333b5(phal chen): bzod la rab tu gnas/ / chos kyi 'byung gnas yin pas na// shin tu brtson pa rab tu tshol// brtson 'grus ldog par mi byed do// sangs rgyas byang chub sgrub par byed// dbyangs tsam gyis//
333b6(phal chen): ni gnas byed pas// byang chub sems la bag tshe med// dbyangs kyis mos pa rab tu 'thob// des ni rgyal ba mnyes par byed// skyes bu la la bsod nams rgyas gyur pas// gser gyi
333b7(phal chen): 'byung gnas chen po rnyed gyur nas/ / brgyan pa'i gnas kyi rgyan du rab spangs nas// de dag lus dang mthun pa'i rgyan du byed// de bzhin mkhas pas chos kyi phul thos na//
334a1(phal chen): sems dang blo yang sa rgya mtshor bsgyur bya shing // ji ltar sngon thos chos rnams rtogs par byed// mi mthun tshul du chos la tshol mi byed// de dag rtogs nas shin tu mthun par spyod/
334a2(phal chen): rnam par mi sgom chos ni gang yang med// de dag chos rnams ji bzhin mthun byed cing // de bzhin de ni khong du chud par byed// mkhas pa'i sems ni rnam dag skyer 'gyur te// dga' ba'i sems
334a3(phal chen): yid rnams dang gsal ba ste/ / chos kyi yid la bdag nyid che ba brtson// rten cing 'brel 'byung chos la rab tu 'jug/ chos rnams mnyam pa nyid la de brtson te// dngos po rnam par bsgom la
334a4(phal chen): mngon par brtson/ / rgyal ba'i mdzod dang 'gal bar mi byed de// chos rnams mi mnyam med par rab tu shes// de ni bsam pa mthar thug rab brtan pas// rgyal ba'i byang chub
334a5(phal chen): ji bzhin rab tu sbyong / / ri rab bzhin du mi g.yo brtan pa yis// de yi bsam pa byang chub mchog la rten// mnyam gzhag sems dang ldan pas de brtson te// brtson 'grus ldan pa'i
334a6(phal chen): yid kyis rab tu spyod/ / bskal pa stong du spyad pa spyod byed kyang // de yi brtson 'grus 'jig par mi 'gyur ro// 'di dag chos la yang dag de 'jug ste// rgyal ba'i rtog bya'i gting
334a7(phal chen): yang rab tu rnyed/ / chos nyid zhi ba rab tu thob gyur pas// de la 'jum pa'i yid byed gang yang med// dpe zla med pas ji skad gsungs pa ltar// de ni chos rnams mnyam pa nyid du//
334b1(phal chen): byed// mi mnyam tshul du bzod pa mi skyed de// ye shes mnyam nyid yongs su rdzogs par sgrub// bde bar gshegs pas mthun par gang gsungs pas// de dag bzod pa'i sgo
334b2(phal chen): nas rab tu 'grub/ / chos rnams 'jig dang ldan pa ma yin te// chos nyid ji bzhin de 'dra rab tu shes// lha gnas 'di lha'i bu rnams 'dir 'dus pa// sum cu rtsa gsum gnas su lha/
334b3(phal chen): rnams skyes gyur pa// de dag zil dngar sna tshogs rnam pa gzhan dang gzhan// de dag 'khar bar snod gcig mngon spyod phrad gyur na// zil dngar zhim pa de dag 'ongs pa ma yin te//
334b4(phal chen): phyogs bcu kun nas zil dngar stobs pa myed// las rnams ci lta ci bzhin lha rnams de ltar za// de la skye ba med de bza' bar med pa min// de bzhin byang chub sems dpa'i sems rab
334b5(phal chen): mngon skyes kyang / / de la rdul cha'i chos kyang skyes par gyur pa med// ma skyes gang yin chos de rnams yang 'gag pa med// dam pa'i chos kyi rkyen brten mkhas pa rab tu zhugs
334b6(phal chen): ma 'gago gang yin mi zad chos rgyud de dang de/ / chos nyid 'jo yi tshul la rab tu gnas pa yin// tha dad med pa'i chos dbyings 'di la rab tu 'jug/ 'jig rten tha dad med pa'i rgyud kyi
334b7(phal chen): tshul yang shes/ / de bzhin nyid mnyam 'jig rten zhi ba'i gzhir gyur pa// gzhi med tha dad med pa'i yang dag mtha' shes te// smon lam rdo rje'i rang bzhin 'gro la phan phyir 'debs/
335a1(phal chen): rgyal sras de ni bde gshegs mkhyen la'ang mngon chags med// de ni dben gzhol sangs rgyas chos rnams ston par byed// chos kyi shugs las 'od kyang g.yo bar
335a2(phal chen): 'gyur ba med/ / brda dang grangs kyi tshul gyis mngon par 'du byed de// 'jig rten snying brtser smon lam dam pa rab tu 'debs// smon lam 'debs la gnas kyang stobs bcu ldan pa ste/
335a3(phal chen): 'gro ba ma lus kun la de ni gnas pa med// mkhas pa'i ye shes yongs su len dang 'dong ba spangs// chos dang chos kyi man ngag rnam pa'i tshul la mkhas// 'di ni bzod pa'i ngam
335a4(phal chen): pa ma skyes chos can te/ / des ni chos rnams zad med zad par mi 'gyur ro// mi skye'i tshul gyis yongs su gdams bya'i chos kyi dbyings// de bzhin nyid las brtan pa rnam par 'gyur ba med//
335a5(phal chen): rgyal sras byang chub don du bzod pa 'di gnas pa// de la phyogs kun sangs rgyas mtha' yas lung yang ston// rgyal sras de la sangs rgyas mkhyen pas dbang bskur mdzad// phyogs bcu
335a6(phal chen): kun nas rab tu snang bar mngon du gnas/ / de dag chos kun rab zhi rtag tu zhi ba'i sems// mngon par sgrub cing dge ba kun la 'gro ba 'god// dus gsum chos rnams kun gyi mtshan nyid de
335a7(phal chen): 'dra bas/ / mtshan rnams yongs su dag byas sems can 'dul ba byed// sgyu ma lta bu'i chos rnams nges par sus rtogs pa// de dag 'jig rten sna tshogs du ma tshogs du ma rtogs byed cing // /
335b1(phal chen): 'jig rten sna tshogs sgyu tshul yang dag rtogs byas nas// las yangs shin tu bsags pas rnam pa sna tshogs pa// sems las las kyi rnam pa du ma 'byung bar 'gyur//
335b2(phal chen): de bas 'jig rten sems ni sgyu ma lta bur bstan// de dag rnam brtags sgyu ma 'dra bas nub par 'gyur// srid pa'i lam rgyud ma lus sgyu 'dra yang dag min// ji ltar sgyu ma'i
335b3(phal chen): rnam pa byin brlabs byas pa'i gzugs/ / lam gyi bzhi mdor 'jig rten phal gyi nang bstan pa// 'gro bas mthong na de la kun kyang mos pa skyed// sgyu mas 'jig rten las ni gang yang
335b4(phal chen): 'grub mi 'gyur/ / de bzhin 'gro ba ji snyed gang rnams yod pa dag/ sgyu ma'i rang bzhin lta bu ma skyes chos nyid de// dngos yod dngos med de bzhin yad dang med pa dang // skal ba
335b5(phal chen): mi ma'am tshul gyis 'gre rgyud rab tu sten/ / sgyu ma'i tshul rnams shes nas sems can yongs su 'grel// sgyu ma lta bu yin par sems can khong du chud// sems can sgyu 'dra de bzhin sgyu ma sem
335b6(phal chen): can 'dra/ / sems can med cing sgyu ma 'dra bar 'jig rten shes// sems can zhing dang chos dang de bzhin dus gsum dang // 'jig rten thams cad sgyu ma'i rnam par rab tu 'byed// sgyu/
335b7(phal chen): ma'i rnam pa lta bu chos rnams rab rdzogs pas// 'jig rten ma lus 'di dag sgyu ma'i rnam par shes// skyes pa dag dang de bzhin bud med rogs po dag/ bu mo de bzhin rnam par dul ba nye bar
336a1(phal chen): ston/ glang po rta dang baglang phyugs dang shing rnams dang // me tog 'bras bu bzang dang ldan pa'i 'tsho yang ston// thabs kyi rnam pa sna tshogs mang bar sgyu ba'i
336a2(phal chen): sems/ / sna tshogs gnas la'ang sgyu ma yongs su gnas pa med// sgyu ma dben la gzhol zhing shin tu zhi ba yang // 'jig rten rnam par rtog pa rnam pa mang po ston// de bzhin rgyal sras
336a3(phal chen): btsun pa rigs dang ldan pa'i rnams/ / 'jig rten sgyu ma sna tshogs ci bzhin ston par byed// sgom dang rnam par sgom pa'i dngos po'i sems kyang med// dngos po dngos med sgyu ma ji bzhin
336a4(phal chen): rab tu shes/ / zhing dang sems can chos kyi rnam pa mang por bcas// las rnams sna tshogs rnam pas yongs su bsags pa la// gnas par mi byed mngon par chags pa de bzhin med/
336a5(phal chen): chags med mtha' yi sgyu ma'i tshul ni des shes so// de ltar rgyal sras mkhas pa'i rnams// rab tu zhi la dga' zhing spros pa med pa ste// gnas med sa dang yang dag ldan// chos dbyi
336a6(phal chen): gnas la de dag rab tu zhugs/ / de dag chos nyid rtogs pa ste// brtan pa de dag rgyal ba'i sku skyes sras yin no// 'du shes sgyu ma mkhas pa ste// 'gro ba thams cad 'du shes 'dra
336a7(phal chen): par shes/ / smig rgyu 'du shes 'dra ba ste// 'gro ba thams cad 'du shes phyin ci log/ 'du shes rnam phye mkhas pa ste// de ni 'gro kun 'du shes spangs pa yin// sems
336b1(phal chen): can sna tshogs khong du chud/ / 'jig rten kun gyi sna tshogs rnam pa kun dang bral// 'jig rten 'du shes rab tu shes// 'jig rten 'du shes med min 'du shes ldan// phyogs rnams
336b2(phal chen): 'du shes 'dra ba ste/ / sems can mtha' yas 'du shes rnam pa sna tshogs yin// ma nor mig dang ldan pa'i rnams// 'jig rten sna tshogs 'du shes rab tu mthong // 'jig rten
336b3(phal chen): smig rgyu 'dra ba ste/ / 'du shes sna tshogs rnam pas 'jig rten rnam par bkod// 'jig rten 'du shes gnas pa ste// de dag phyin ci log gsum rnam par spangs// ji ltar smig
336b4(phal chen): rgyu'i tshogs kyi rnams/ / 'gro ba rnams la chu yi rnam pa dmigs par snang // de la chu ni yod min yang // chu yi 'du shes rnam par rab tu slu// de bzhin 'jig rten thams
336b5(phal chen): cad kyang / / khams gsum lam rgyud rnam pa sna tshogs mtha' yas te// 'du shes rnam pa smig rgyu bzhin// 'du shes rnam pa chu zla bzhin// chags med yid ldan spyod yul
336b6(phal chen): mtha' yas so/ / 'du shes thams cad rnam par spangs// chags med ye shes ldan zhing spros pa med pa'i rnams// 'gro ba 'du shes chags gyur pa// 'du shes bslus las brtan
336b7(phal chen): pa 'grel par byed/ / nga rgyal rlom dang dregs pa spangs// 'du shes thams cad bsal cing 'jig rten 'dren pa byed// mi zang zad pa rdzogs pa'i rnams// bden pa zad mi shes
